msg:Hainan Island Self-driving: Dongfang. Family rooms are not enough for parents, so two standard rooms are booked.

About facilities
Parking: The hotel is one of the few newly opened hotels in the city. There are public parking spaces on the ground and the hotel's exclusive underground parking lot. No charge.
Room: Standard room. Lucky bamboo tea set. The toilet flushes normally in the bathroom sink. The floor drain does not smell. The shower head is hot and the water is normal. It is equipped with disposable full toiletries (toothbrush/shaving/care bag/shower cap). There is a small refrigerator in the room. The TV screen is large and the channels are clear. Because one person lives in the standard room, it is changed to a double bed. The bed is also very clean.

About hygiene. The newly opened sight is very hygienic.

About environment. The external environment is adjacent to the road. If you don't want to be disturbed, ask the front desk for a quiet room in advance. The internal environment is normal and reasonable.

About service. There is a greeting at the front desk when checking in and checking out. The service attitude of the dinner restaurant is normal.

About catering. Check-in discount dinner is 15% off. The radish tastes good. The room breakfast has everything. You can eat enough~
